# Testo Voynich decodificato (ipotesi giudeo-italiana)
# Direzione: RTL
# Formato: folio | EVA | italiano

=== f1r [sezione T] ===
  fachys ykal ar ataiin shol shory cthres y kor sholdy
  → itskosg tsets ts dppsls tski tstski irtklo ts tse tsetski

  sory ckhar or y kair chtaiin shar are cthar cthar dan
  → tstsi tskeo ts ts tpse dppslko tski rts tsklo tsklo dse

  syaiir sheky or ykaiin shod cthoary cthes daraiin sa
  → tppstsi tserki ts dppsets eski tstssklo irklo dppstse si

  ooiin oteey oteos roloty cthar daiin otaiin or okan
  → dppss tsrrls isrls tslstst tsklo dppse dppsls ts dses

  dair y chear cthaiin cphar cfhaiin
  → tpse ts tsrko dppsklo tskzo dppskgo

  ydaraishy
  → tskipstsets

  odar o y shol cphoy oydar sh s cfhoaiin shodary
  → tses s ts tski tsskzo tsetss ki i dppsskgo tstseski

  yshey shody okchoy otchol chocthy oschy dain chor kos
  → tsrkits tseski tsskoes tskols tsklosko tskois dpse tsko ise

  daiin shos cfhol shody
  → dppse iski tskgo tseski

  dain os teody
  → dpse is tsesrl

  ydain cphesaiin ol s cphey ytain shoshy cphodales
  → dpsets dppsirkzo ts i tsrkzo dpslts tskiski irtseskzo

  oksho kshoy otairin oteol okan shodain sckhey daiin
  → skies tsskie dptpsls tsrls dses dpseski tsrkeoi dppse

  shoy ckhey kodaiin cphy cphodaiils cthey she oldain d
  → tsski tsrkeo dppsese tskzo itppseskzo tsrklo rki dpsets e

  dain oiin chol odaiin chodain chdy okain dan cthy kod
  → dpse dpps tsko dppses dpsesko tseko dpses dse tsklo ese

  daiin shckhey ckeor chor shey kol chol chol kor chal
  → dppse tsrkeoki tsreo tsko tsrki tse tsko tsko tse tsko

  sho chol shodan kshy kchy dor chodaiin sho kchom
  → ski tsko dseski tskie tskoe tse dppsesko ski mskoe

  ycho tchey chokain sheo pshol dydyd cthy daicthy
  → skots tsrkol dpsesko srki tskiz etsetse tsklo tsklopse

  yto shol she kodshey cphealy dasain dain ckhyds
  → slts tski rki tsrkiese tstsrkzo dpsise dpse ietskeo

  dchar shcthaiin okaiir chey rchy potol cthols dlocta
  → tskoe dppskloki tppses tsrko tskot tslsz itsklo sloste

  shok chor chey dain ckhey
  → eski tsko tsrko dpse tsrkeo

  otol daiiin
  → tsls dpppse

  cpho shaiin shokcheey chol tshodeesy shey pydeey chy ro d
  → skzo dppski tsrrkoeski tsko tsirreskil tsrki tsrretsz tsko st e

  doin chol dain cthal dar shear kaiin dar shey cthar
  → dpse tsko dpse tsklo tse tsrki dppse tse tsrki tsklo

  choo kaiin shoaiin okol daiin far cthol daiin ctholdar
  → ssko dppse dppsski tses dppse tsg tsklo dppse tsetsklo

  ycheey okay oky daiin okchey kokaiin chol kchy dal
  → tsrrkots tsses tses dppse tsrkoes dppsese tsko tskoe tse

  deeo shody koshey cthy okchey keey keey dal chtor
  → srre tseski tsrkise tsklo tsrkoes tsrre tsrre tse tslko

  eo chol chok choty chotey
  → sr tsko esko tslsko tsrlsko

  dchaiin
  → dppskoe


=== f1v [sezione H] ===
  kchsy chadaiin ololtchey char cfhar am
  → tsikoe dppsesko tsrkoltsts tsko tskgo ms

  yteeay char or ochydcho lkody okodar chody
  → tssrrlts tsko ts skoetskos tseset tseses tsesko

  do ckhy ckho ckhy shydksheey cthy kotchody dal
  → se tskeo skeo tskeo tsrrkieetski tsklo tseskolse tse

  dol chokeo dair damsochey chokody
  → tse sresko tpse tsrkosimse tsesesko

  potoy shol dair cphoaldar chey tody otoaiin shoshy
  → tsslsz tski tpse tsetsskzo tsrko tsesl dppssls tskiski

  choky chol cthol shol okaldolchey chodo lol chy cthy
  → tsesko tsko tsklo tski tsrkotsetses sesko tst tsko tsklo

  qo ol choeee cheol dol ctheyykol dol dolo ykol do lchody
  → sa ts rrrsko tsrko tse tsetstsrklo tse stse tsets se tseskot

  okol shol kol kechy chol kychol cthol chody chol daiin
  → tses tski tse tskore tsko tskotse tsklo tsesko tsko dppse

  shor okol chol dol ky darshol dchor otcho dar shody
  → tski tses tsko tse tse tskitse tskoe skols tse tseski

  taor chotchey dal chodyschody pol chodar
  → tssl tsrkolsko tse tseskoitsesko tsz tsesko


=== f2r [sezione H] ===
  kydainy ypchol daiin otchalypchaiin ckholsy
  → tsdpsetse tskozts dppse dppskoztstskols tsitskeo

  dorchorychkar sshor cthy cth
  → tsekotstskotse tskii tsklo klo

  qotaiincthey ychor chy ydychaiin
  → tsrklodppslsa tskots tsko dppskotsets

  chaindychtod dycphy dalschokaiin d
  → eslkotsedpsko tskzotse dppseskoitse e

  otochor alshodaiinchol danytchaiin dan
  → tskosls tskodppseskits dppskoltsdse dse

  saiin dainddkol sorytoldydchol dchy cthy
  → dppsi tseeedpse tskoetsetsltstsi tskoe tsklo

  shor ckhy daiinychol dan
  → tski tskeo tskotsdppse dse

  kydain shaiin qoy s shol fodanyksh olsheey daiildy
  → dpsetse dppski tssa i tski kietsdsesg tsrrkits tsetppse

  dlssho kol sheey qokey ykody sochol yky dain daiirol
  → skiite tse tsrrki tsresa tsesets tskosi tsets dpse tstppse

  qoky cholaiin shol sheky daiincthey keol saiin saiin
  → tsesa dppstsko tski tserki tsrklodppse tsre dppsi dppsi

  ychain dal chy dalor shan danolsaiin sheey ckhor
  → dpskots tse tsko tstse dski dppsitsdse tsrrki tskeo

  okol chy chor cthor yor an chansaiin chety chyky sal
  → tses tsko tsko tsklo tsts ds dppsidsko tslrko tsetsko tsi

  sho ykeey chey daiin chcthy
  → ski tsrrets tsrko dppse tskloko


=== f2v [sezione H] ===
  kooiin cheo pchor otaiin o dain chordair shty
  → dppsse srko tskoz dppsls s dpse tpsetsko tslki

  kcho kchy sho shol qotcho loeees qotychor daiin
  → skoe tskoe ski tski skolsa irrrst tskotslsa dppse

  otchy chor lshy chol chody chodainchcthy daiin
  → tskols tsko tskit tsko tsesko tsklokodpsesko dppse

  sho cholo cheor chodaiin
  → ski stsko tsrko dppsesko

  kchor shy daiiin chckhoys shey dor chol daiin
  → tskoe tski dpppse itsskeoko tsrki tse tsko dppse

  dor chol chor chol keol chy chtydaiin otchor chan
  → tse tsko tsko tsko tsre tsko dppsetslko tskols dsko

  daiin chotchey qoteeey chokeoschees chr cheaiin
  → dppse tsrkolsko tsrrrlsa irrkoisresko tko dppsrko

  chokoishe chor cheol chol dolody
  → rkipsesko tsko tsrko tsko tsestse


=== f3r [sezione H] ===
  tsheos qopal chol cthol daimm
  → isrkil tszsa tsko tsklo mmpse

  ycheor chor dam qotcham cham
  → tsrkots tsko mse mskolsa msko

  ochor qocheor chol daiin cthy
  → tskos tsrkosa tsko dppse tsklo

  schey chor chal cham cham cho
  → tsrkoi tsko tsko msko msko sko

  qokol chololy s cham cthol
  → tsesa tststsko i msko tsklo

  ychtaiin chor cthom otal dam
  → dppslkots tsko msklo tsls mse

  otchol qodaiin chom shom damo
  → tskols dppsesa msko mski smse

  ysheor chor chol oky damo
  → tsrkits tsko tsko tses smse

  sho or sheoldam otchody ol
  → ski ts msetsrki tseskols ts

  ydas chol cthom
  → isets tsko msklo

  pcheol shol sols sheol shey
  → tsrkoz tski itsi tsrki tsrki

  okadaiin qokchor qoschodam octhy
  → dppseses tskoesa mseskoisa tsklos

  qokeey qot shey qokody qokchey cheody
  → tsrresa lsa tsrki tsesesa tsrkoesa tsesrko

  chor qodair okeey qokeey
  → tsko tpsesa tsrres tsrresa

  tsheoarom shor or chor olchsy chom otchomoporar
  → mstssrkil tski ts tsko tsikots msko tstszsmskols

  oteol chol s cheol ekshy qokeom qokol daiinsoleeg
  → tsrls tsko i tsrko tskier msresa tsesa brrtsidppse

  soeom okeom yteody qokeeo dal sam
  → msrsi msres tsesrlts srresa tse msi

  pcheoldom shodaiin qopchor qopol opchol qotyotolom
  → msetsrkoz dppseski tskozsa tszsa tskozs mstslstslsa

  otchor ol cheor qoeor dair qoteol qosaiinchor cthy
  → tskols ts tsrko tsrsa tpse tsrlsa tskodppsisa tsklo

  ycheor chol odaiin chol s aiin okolor am
  → tsrkots tsko dppses tsko i dpps tstses ms


=== f3v [sezione H] ===
  koaiin cphor qotoy sha ckhol ykoaiin s oly
  → dppsse tskzo tsslsa ski tskeo dppssets i tsts

  daiidy qoteeol okchor okor olytol dol dar
  → tseppse tsrrlsa tskoes tses tsltsts tse tse

  okom chol shol seees chom cheeykam okai
  → mses tsko tski irrri msko msetsrrko pses

  qodar ees eey kcheol okal do r chear een
  → tsesa irr tsrr tsrkoe tses se t tsrko drr

  yeeear otchal eeor eear ckhy
  → tsrrrts tskols tsrr tsrr tskeo

  or cheor kor chodaly chom
  → ts tsrko tse tstsesko msko

  tchor otcham chor cfham s
  → tskol mskols tsko mskgo i

  ykchy kchom chor chekeol oka
  → tskoets mskoe tsko tsrerko ses

  ytcheear okeol cthodoaly chor cthy
  → tsrrkolts tsres tstssesklo tsko tsklo

  ochor daiin qokshol daiim chol okary
  → tskos dppse tskiesa mppse tsko tstses

  sho shockho ckhy tchor chodaiin chom
  → ski skeoski tskeo tskol dppsesko msko

  osh chodair ytchy tchor kcham s
  → kis tpsesko tskolts tskol mskoe i

  shar shkaiin qokchy yty cthal chky
  → tski dppseki tskoesa tslts tsklo tseko

  dain sheam yteam
  → dpse msrki msrlts


=== f4r [sezione H] ===
  kodalchy chpady sheol ol sheey qoteydoiin chor ytoy
  → tskotsese tseszko tsrki ts tsrrki dppsetsrlsa tsko tsslts

  dchor chol shol cthol shtchy chaiinschoraiin chom
  → tskoe tsko tski tsklo tskolki dppstskoidppsko msko

  otchol chol chy chaiin qotaiindaiin shain
  → tskols tsko tsko dppsko dppsedppslsa dpski

  qotchol chy yty daiin okaiin cthy
  → tskolsa tsko tslts dppse dppses tsklo

  pydaiin qotchy dy tydy
  → dppsetsz tskolsa tse tsetsl

  chor shytchy dy tcheay
  → tsko tskoltski tse tssrkol

  qotaiin cthol daiin cthom
  → dppslsa tsklo dppse msklo

  shor shol shol cthy cpholdy
  → tski tski tski tsklo tsetskzo

  daiin ckhochy tchy koraiin
  → dppse tskoskeo tskol dppstse

  odal shor shyshol cphaiin
  → tses tski tskitski dppskzo

  qotchoiin sheyr qoty
  → dppskolsa ttsrki tslsa

  soiin chaiin chaiin
  → dppsi dppsko dppsko

  daiin cthey
  → dppse tsrklo


=== f4v [sezione H] ===
  pchooiin ksheo kchoy chopchy doldsdlod
  → dppsskoz srkie tsskoe tskozsko esteietse

  ol chey chy cthy shkchor sheo cheorycholdy
  → ts tsrko tsko tsklo tskoeki srki tsetskotstsrko

  sho sho chaiin shaiin daiin qodaiino ar am
  → ski ski dppsko dppski dppse sdppsesa ts ms

  qokshy qocthy choteol daiin ctheychoaiin
  → tskiesa tsklosa tsrlsko dppse dppsskotsrklo

  shor sheey cto otoiin shey qotchoiinchodain
  → tski tsrrki slo dppsls tsrki dpseskodppskolsa

  ytchoy shokchy cphody
  → tsskolts tskoeski tseskzo

  torchy sheeor chor shokchy cphydy
  → tskotsl tsrrki tsko tskoeski tsetskzo

  olaen chor cthol sho otor cthory
  → drsts tsko tsklo ski tsls tstsklo

  qooko iiincheom chcthy shoky daiin
  → sessa msrkodppp tskloko tseski dppse

  otaiin sheo okeody chol chokeody
  → dppsls srki tsesres tsko tsesresko

  sho kcheor shody shtaiin qotol daiin
  → ski tsrkoe tseski dppslki tslsa dppse

  qokoy sho okeol s keey shar char ody
  → tssesa ski tsres i tsrre tski tsko tses

  shody s cheor chokody shodaiin qoty
  → tseski i tsrko tsesesko dppseski tslsa

  ochody chykey chtody
  → tseskos tsretsko tseslko


=== f5r [sezione H] ===
  kshody fchoy chkoy oaiin oar olsy chody dkshy dy
  → tseskie tsskog tsseko dppss tss tsits tsesko tskiee tse

  ochey okey qokaiin sho ckhoy cthey chey okaor otol
  → tsrkos tsres dppsesa ski tsskeo tsrklo tsrko tsses tsls

  qoaiin otan chy daiin oteeen cho cthy otchy qotcho dy
  → dppssa dsls tsko dppse drrrls sko tsklo tskols skolsa tse

  otain sheody chan s cheor chocthy
  → dpsls tsesrki dsko i tsrko tsklosko

  tshy shody qoaiin cholols sho qotcheo daiin shodaiin
  → tskil tseski dppssa itstsko ski srkolsa dppse dppseski

  sho cheor chey qoeeey qoykeeey qoeor cthy shotshy dy
  → ski tsrko tsrko tsrrrsa tsrrretssa tsrsa tsklo tskilski tse

  qotoeey keey cheo kchy shody
  → tsrrslsa tsrre srko tskoe tseski


=== f5v [sezione H] ===
  kocheor chor ytchey pshod chols chodaiin ytoiiin daiin
  → tsrkose tsko tsrkolts eskiz itsko dppsesko dpppslts dppse

  dchol sy chol otaiin dain cthor chots ychopordg
  → tskoe tsi tsko dppsls dpse tsklo ilsko betszskots

  qotcho ytor daiin daiin otchor daiir qo darchor do
  → skolsa tslts dppse dppse tskols tppse sa tskotse se

  qotor shees otol ykoiin shol daiin cthor okchy taiin
  → tslsa irrki tsls dppsets tski dppse tsklo tskoes dppsl

  shokeeol chor cheotol otchol daiin dal chol chotaiin
  → tsrreski tsko tslsrko tskols dppse tse tsko dppslsko

  otol chol dairodg
  → tsls tsko bestpse


=== f6r [sezione H] ===
  foar y shol cholor cphol chor chckhchopchol otcham
  → tssg ts tski tstsko tskzo tsko tskozskokeoko mskols

  daiin chckhy chor chor kar cthycthor chotols
  → dppse tskeoko tsko tsko tse tsklotsklo itslsko

  poeear kshor choky os cheoeesykeor ytaiin dar
  → tsrrsz tskie tsesko is tsretsirrsrko dppslts tse

  dar cho s sheor chocthy otchamyaiir chy
  → tse sko i tsrki tsklosko tppstsmskols tsko

  tar okoiin shees ytaly cthaiinodam
  → tsl dppses irrki tstslts msesdppsklo

  or al daiin ckham okom cthaiinydaiin
  → ts ts dppse mskeo mses dppsetsdppsklo

  daiin qodaiin cho s chol okaiin s
  → dppse dppsesa sko i tsko dppses i

  ychol ckhor pchar sheo ckhaiin
  → tskots tskeo tskoz srki dppskeo

  dar sheeol skaiiodar otaiin chory
  → tse tsrrki tsesppsei dppsls tstsko

  tchor ctheod chy shor odshe od
  → tskol esrklo tsko tski rkies es

  ychar olchad ol chokaiin
  → tskots eskots ts dppsesko

  or shol cthom chor cthy
  → ts tski msklo tsko tsklo

  qocthol qodaiin cthy
  → tsklosa dppsesa tsklo

  ysho taiin y kaiim
  → skits dppsl ts mppse


=== f6v [sezione H] ===
  koar y sar oheekar qoar shor chapchy s chear char otchy
  → tsse ts tsi tserrks tssa tski tskozsko i tsrko tsko tskols

  oees chor chckhy qoekchar cheas odaiin kchey chor chaiin
  → irrs tsko tskeoko tskoersa isrko dppses tsrkoe tsko dppsko

  qoair ckhy chol oochockhy chekchoy ckhy okolrychos
  → tpssa tskeo tsko tskeoskoss tsskoerko tskeo iskotsttses

  y shckhy ytchoy sos y dady dchy dey okodyytody
  → ts tskeoki tsskolts isi ts tsese tskoe tsre tsesltstseses

  dair cshe chodam dam okor oty doldom
  → tpse rkio msesko mse tses tsls msetse

  tchody shocthol chocthey s
  → tseskol tskloski tsrklosko i

  ychos ychol daiin cthol dol
  → iskots tskots dppse tsklo tse

  ychor chor okchey qokom
  → tskots tsko tsrkoes msesa

  oeeo dal chor cthom s
  → srrs tse tsko msklo i

  qokche ychear kchdy
  → rkoesa tsrkots tsekoe

  lor char otam cthom dy
  → tst tsko msls msklo tse

  ytchos shy qokam cthy
  → iskolts tski msesa tsklo

  yodaiin cthy s chor oees or
  → dppsests tsklo i tsko irrs ts

  qokor chol cthol tchalody
  → tsesa tsko tsklo tsestskol

  chockhy s os chy sain or
  → tskeosko i is tsko dpsi ts

  ochy cthar cthar cthy
  → tskos tsklo tsklo tsklo

  y chaiir ckhal cthodam dy
  → ts tppsko tskeo msesklo tse

  ytcho cthol ches cthor
  → skolts tsklo irko tsklo

  ocholy kchos chy dor
  → tstskos iskoe tsko tse

  dchor choldar okol daiin
  → tskoe tsetsko tses dppse

  ycheor chor octham
  → tsrkots tsko msklos


=== f7r [sezione H] ===
  fchodaiin shopchey qkoshey qoos sheey chorochy
  → dppseskog tsrkozski tsrkisea issa tsrrki tskostsko

  dcheey keor shor dolddchey kchey otchy cheody
  → tsrrkoe tsre tski tsrkoeetse tsrkoe tskols tsesrko

  oeeees cheodaiin sheeyytcheey qotchy chald
  → irrrrs dppsesrko tsrrkoltstsrrki tskolsa etsko

  qokcho cho lochey daiinychey kchosodaiin
  → skoesa sko tsrkost tsrkotsdppse dppsesiskoe

  oaiirotaiin
  → dppslstppss

  ksholochey qotoees chkoldyotchor choaiin
  → tsrkostskie irrslsa tskolstsetseko dppssko

  dshoy cthol chol otchol dainshody shol chotchy
  → tsskie tsklo tsko tskols tseskidpse tski tskolsko

  okchey deeeese choty qokchyshol keey choty dain
  → tsrkoes rirrrre tslsko tskitskoesa tsrre tslsko dpse

  qokechy olchoiin chol cpheyshckhy chochy kchod
  → tskoresa dppskots tsko tskeokitsrkzo tskosko eskoe

  schain chor daiin chckhy
  → dpskoi tsko dppse tskeoko


=== f7v [sezione H] ===
  polyshy shey tchody qopchy otshol dy daiin tshodody
  → tskitstsz tsrki tseskol tskozsa tskils tse dppse tseseskil

  chochy cthy daiin qoky chcphhy daiin cthol cthy cthd
  → tskosko tsklo dppse tsesa tskkzoko dppse tsklo tsklo eklo

  qokchy dykchy chkeey kshy ky ty dor cheey ol cheol dy
  → tskoesa tskoetse tsrreko tskie tse tsl tse tsrrko ts tsrko tse

  choteeen oeear choschy dain sho kshy shol deees dol
  → drrrlsko tsrrs tskoisko dpse ski tskie tski irrre tse

  dchodaiin qotchy cheey tcheey
  → dppseskoe tskolsa tsrrko tsrrkol

  kchor sheod sheodaiin shodaiin oksholshol dais qos
  → tskoe esrki dppsesrki dppseski tskitskies ipse isa

  okshodeeen chor cheor odaiin shotchodol dol dor aiin
  → drrreskies tsko tsrko dppses tseskolski tse tse dpps

  qoteeeo rcho cheeody qotchey teyokchor daiin
  → srrrlsa skot tsesrrko tsrkolsa tskoestsrl dppse

  sho keeo daiir chokchy dor deol dydol daiin
  → ski srre tppse tskoesko tse tsre tsetse dppse


=== f8r [sezione H] ===
  pshol chor otshal chopycphol chody shy cfhodar shor
  → tskiz tsko tskils tskzotszsko tsesko tski tseskgo tski

  tchty sh kcheals shookche do dchy dain al
  → tslkol ki itsrkoe rkoesski se tskoe dpse ts

  chodar shy rychodaiin shokchy chor dy
  → tsesko tski dppseskotst tskoeski tsko tse

=== f112v [sezione S] ===

  odaiin shey qokas aleey chy
  → dppses tsrki isesa tsrrts tsko

  oqokain al shey qokar okaral okey shcphhy oteey o okar okydy
  → dpsesas ts tsrki tsesa tstses tsres tskkzoki tsrrls s tses tsetses

  osain shky qorain chckhey qokey lkechy okeey okal chedkaly
  → dpsis tseki dpstsa tsrkeoko tsresa tskoret tsrres tses tstseerko

  sykar ain olkeey dain choy qokar chey dain y otan otain oly
  → tsetsi dps tsrrets dpse tssko tsesa tsrko dpse ts dsls dpsls tsts

  sosar shey qokey okeolan chey qol or cheey qor aram ol lkan
  → tsisi tsrki tsresa dstsres tsrko tsa ts tsrrko tsa msts ts dset

  sodal chal chcthy chckhy qol ain ary
  → tsesi tsko tskloko tskeoko tsa dps tsts
